[30;1m881 | [0m[35m### Debugging Configuration[0m
[30;1m882 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m883 | [0m[35mFor the entries in `[bumpver:file_patterns]` you can expect two failure modes:[0m
[30;1m884 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m885 | [0m[35m- False negative: A pattern *will not* match a version number in the associated file *which it shoul[0m
[30;1m886 | [0m[35m- False positive: A pattern *will* match something it *should not match* (less likely).[0m
